p6dof_object_types

   jet_engine_type   TurbofanFighter   P6DOF_JET_ENGINE

# -----------------------------------------------------------------------

      # Thrust Offset 
      # The thrust offset is used to specify the position at which to apply thrust
      # produced by the engine.  It is the offset along the length (x) of the engine from
      # the center of the engine.

      thrust_offset     -8.000000 ft

      # -----------------------------------------------------------------------

      # Inoperative Reference Area 
      # This is used to denote the reference area when the engine is inoperative.
      # If defined, it implies that there will be drag created by the specified area
      # with a CD = 1.

      inop_ref_area     7.068583 ft^2

      # -----------------------------------------------------------------------

      # Thrust specific fuel consumption
      # The values define the fuel burn rate (lbs of fuel burned per hour)
      # per lb of thrust produced. Three conditions are supported (idle,
      # mil power, and afterburner) and intermediate values are interpolated.
      
      tsfc_idle_pph        0.750
      tsfc_mil_pph         0.750
      tsfc_ab_pph          2.000
      
      # -----------------------------------------------------------------------

      # Thrust ratings (these are used as a reference to compute percent thrust)
      # Actual thrust values are defined in the tables below
      
      rated_thrust_idle    2000.00 lbf
      rated_thrust_mil     16000.00 lbf
      rated_thrust_ab      26000.00 lbf
      
      # -----------------------------------------------------------------------
      
      # Engine response (spin-up/spin-down)
      
      # Engine spin-up and spin-down rates when not using afterburner
      spin_up_mil_per_sec     0.2
      spin_down_mil_per_sec   0.25

      # Engine spin-up and spin-down rates when using afterburner
      spin_up_ab_per_sec      0.5
      spin_down_ab_per_sec    0.4
